REUTERS/Arnd Wiegmann/File Photo"></div><div class="BackdropImage-image-a7Ah5 AutoSizeImage-container-19DRs" role="img" aria-label="FILE PHOTO: The logo of Swiss drugmaker Roche is seen at its headquarters in Basel, Switzerland February 1, 2018. REUTERS/Arnd Wiegmann/File Photo" title="FILE PHOTO: The logo of Swiss drugmaker Roche is seen at its headquarters in Basel, Switzerland February 1, 2018. REUTERS/Arnd Wiegmann/File Photo"></div></div></div><div class="Slideshow-expand-button-2c_q7"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 18 18"><path d="M16.293 1H12.5a.5.5 0 1 1 0-1h5a.5.5 0 0 1 .5.5v5a.5.5 0 1 1-1 0V1.707l-4.146 4.147a.5.5 0 0 1-.708-.708L16.293 1zM1 16.293l4.146-4.147a.5.5 0 0 1 .708.708L1.707 17H5.5a.5.5 0 1 1 0 1h-5a.5.5 0 0 1-.5-.5v-5a.5.5 0 1 1 1 0v3.793z"></path></svg></div></figure></button></div><div class="WithCaption-caption-container-Y-li-"><figcaption>FILE PHOTO: The logo of Swiss drugmaker Roche is seen at its headquarters in Basel, Switzerland February 1, 2018. REUTERS/Arnd Wiegmann/File Photo</figcaption></div></figure><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">Roche is one of the main suppliers of diagnostic tests to Britain\xe2\x80\x99s National Health Service (NHS) Test and Trace programme, which was also hit by a glitch last week that delayed the reporting of nearly 16,000 positive tests.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">The timing of Roche\xe2\x80\x99s problems could hardly be worse with new coronavirus infections topping 14,000 a day and hospital admissions at their highest since June. UK Health Minister Matt Hancock said the latest numbers showed the country had a very serious problem on its hands.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">The Swiss company told UK customers on Wednesday that a switch from an old warehouse to a new automated distribution centre had caused an unforeseen technical issue that lead to a very significant drop in its processing capacity.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">Geoff Twist, general manager of Roche Diagnostics UK and Ireland, made a personal apology to customers in a written statement and said he was confident there would be significant improvements in supplies by this weekend.</p><div class="AdSlot__container___2BqUD ArticleBody-ad-slot-83sCj"><div class="AdSlot__creative___aEugP" id="ad_mpu"></div></div><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">\xe2\x80\x9cWe will be well on the way to resolution by the end of next week,\xe2\x80\x9d he said. The company later said in a statement that the issue \xe2\x80\x9chas not and will not affect our ability to supply COVID-19 tests in the UK.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">Experts said the supply disruption was also affecting diabetes tests, magnesium level tests and other materials such as supplies for blood gas analysers which are crucial for the treatment of respiratory illnesses, including COVID-19.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">Allan Wilson, head of the Institute of Biomedical Science, said Roche and NHS staff were working very hard to plug urgent gaps, including by driving around the country to distribute supplies manually, but that would not be tenable for long.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">\xe2\x80\x9cWe can only do that for a few days before it really starts to impact on our ability to do diagnostic tests,\xe2\x80\x9d he said.</p><div class="ArticleBody-slideshow-small-mFJ54"><button type="button" class="FullscreenOverlay-button-1FTU6 Slideshow-inline-image-container-1dktB" aria-label="slideshow"><figure><div class="Slideshow-inline-image-1uoB6"><div class="BackdropImage-container-2S9Qf BackdropImage-branding-2hzhO" style="height:0;padding-bottom:69.23%"><div class="BackdropImage-image-a7Ah5 AutoSizeImage-container-19DRs" role="img"></div></div></div><div class="Slideshow-expand-button-2c_q7"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 18 18"><path d="M16.293 1H12.5a.5.5 0 1 1 0-1h5a.5.5 0 0 1 .5.5v5a.5.5 0 1 1-1 0V1.707l-4.146 4.147a.5.5 0 0 1-.708-.708L16.293 1zM1 16.293l4.146-4.147a.5.5 0 0 1 .708.708L1.707 17H5.5a.5.5 0 1 1 0 1h-5a.5.5 0 0 1-.5-.5v-5a.5.5 0 1 1 1 0v3.793z"></path></svg></div></figure></button><figcaption class="Slideshow-description-447Md">Slideshow <span>( 2 images )</span></figcaption></div><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">Roche said the issue only affected the UK and Ireland. The production of diagnostics products and solutions was not affected and the supply of Roche Pharmaceuticals was unaffected.</p><h2 class="Headline-headline-2FXIq Headline-black-OogpV ArticleBody-heading-3h695">CONTINGENCY PLANS</h2><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">A spokesman for Prime Minister Boris Johnson played down the impact of Roche\xe2\x80\x99s distribution problems on testing.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">\xe2\x80\x9cIt is expected to have little to no impact on COVID testing and Roche are already prioritising the dispatch of tests to ensure uninterrupted supplies,\xe2\x80\x9d he said, echoing a company statement about the issue at its new warehouse.</p><div class="AdSlot__container___2BqUD ArticleBody-ad-slot-83sCj"><div class="AdSlot__creative___aEugP" id="mpu_native"></div></div><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">The Roche warehouse in Newhaven on England\xe2\x80\x99s south coast supplies customers throughout the United Kingdom and Ireland.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">\xe2\x80\x9cThe current backlog is likely to temporarily affect and disrupt services and, unfortunately, at this stage we may not be able to provide a solution to avoid such a temporary disruption,\xe2\x80\x9d Roche said in a letter to UK customers.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">\xe2\x80\x9cOur customers\xe2\x80\x99 contingency plans may need to be activated and we are working with them to help this happen.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">Wilson of the Institute of Biomedical Science said signs of the problems had emerged last week and scheduled deliveries of certain products had not taken place, leading some hospitals and laboratories to ration test kits.</p><div class="AdSlot__container___2BqUD ArticleBody-ad-slot-83sCj"><div class="AdSlot__creative___aEugP" id="mpu_lower"></div></div><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">\xe2\x80\x9cThe frustration is that they seem to have a warehouse full of consumables but are unable to ship them because the logistics system put in place to manage the extraction and identification of consumables and picking them to send them to customers has failed,\xe2\x80\x9d Wilson said.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">The BBC quoted Tom Lewis, lead clinician for pathology at North Devon District Hospital in southwest England, as saying that his hospital had sent instructions that non-urgent blood tests in the community should stop.</p><p class="Paragraph-paragraph-2Bgue ArticleBody-para-TD_9x">Lewis said that without rationing, the hospital risked running out of swabs in three to four days.</p><div><div class="Attribution-attribution-Y5JpY"><p>Additional reporting by Elizabeth Piper and Ludwig Burger; Writing by Estelle Shirbon, Alistair Smout, Guy Faulconbridge; Editing by Mark Potter, David Clarke and Grant McCool</p></div><div class="TrustBadge-trust-badge-20GM8"><p>Our Standards: <a href="http://thomsonreuters.com/en/about-us/trust-principles.html">The Thomson Reuters Trust Principles.</a></p></div></div></div></article></div><div UK Health Minister Matt Hancock said the latest numbers showed the country had a very serious problem on its hands."},{"type":"paragraph","content":"The Swiss company told UK customers on Wednesday that a switch from an old warehouse to a new automated distribution centre had caused an unforeseen technical issue that lead to a very significant drop in its processing capacity."},{"type":"paragraph","content":"Geoff Twist, general manager of Roche Diagnostics UK and Ireland, made a personal apology to customers in a written statement and said he was confident there would be significant improvements in supplies by this weekend."},{"type":"paragraph","content":"\xe2\x80\x9cWe will be well on the way to resolution by the end of next week,\xe2\x80\x9d he said.
